)@@G@@*[@@@@*SDFF*@A@@@@TABLE OF CONTENTS PROCESSOR, "TOC"  @^@@@@4GENERAL INFQH
)@@G@@ORMATION    @G@@@@     TOC IS BASICALLY DESIGNED FOR USE ON THE UNISCOPEQI
)@@G@@ 100.  IT GIVES A @F@@@@ LISTING OF THE TABLE OF CONTENTS OF A PROGRAM FQJ
)@@G@@ILE FORMATTED TO  @G@@@@ BETTER USE THE UNISCOPE SCREEN.  WHEREAS @PRT,TQK
)@@G@@ WILL GIVE THE ELEMENT  @G@@@@ TABLE OF A PROGRAM FILE, TOC CAN LIST THEQL
)@@G@@ ELEMENT TABLE, ENTRY POINT   @F@@@@ TABLE AND THE VARIOUS PROCEDURE TABQM
)@@G@@LES AS WELL.  TOC ALSO HAS THE@G@@@@ ADVANTAGEOUS FEATURE OF PAUSING WHEQN
)@@G@@N THE SCREEN BECOMES FULL TO ALLOW  @F@@@@ THE USER TO EXAMINE THE CONTEQO
)@@G@@NTS OF THE SCREEN BEFORE PROCEEDING @G@@@@ TO THE REST OF THE TABLE BEINQP
)@@G@@G PRINTED.  IN ADDITION, THE USER MAY     @F@@@@ CHANGE OPTIONS OR TERMIQQ
)@@G@@NATE EXECUTION WHENEVER TOC IS PAUSING FOR@ @@@@ A FULL SCREEN OF INFORMQR
)@@G@@ATION.@[@@@@0     @H@@@@     TOC DYNAMICALLY ASSIGNS AND FREES FILES AS QS
)@@G@@NECESSARY, AND WILL LEAVE     @F@@@@ THE USER'S FACILITIES EXACTLY AS THQT
)@@G@@EY WERE BEFORE EXECUTING TOC. @ @@@@4PROCESSOR CALLING SEQUENCE   @C@@@@QU
)@@G@@     TOC IS CALLED IN THE FOLLOWING MANNER:     @[@@@@SPACE @F@@@@0    *QV
)@@G@@********************************************************    @F@@@@0    *QW
)@@G@@                                                       *    @F@@@@0    *QX
)@@G@@    @P*P.TOC[,OPTIONS] FILENAME.[ELTMASK][/VERMASK]    *    @F@@@@0    *QY
)@@G@@                                                       *    @F@@@@0    *QZ
)@@G@@********************************************************    @]@@@@3FILE RA
)@@G@@NAME  @G@@@@      THE FILENAME MAY HAVE QUALIFIERS, F-CYCLES, AND/OR REARB
)@@G@@D/WRITE     @G@@@@ KEYS IF THEY EXIST ON THE FILE.  THE EFFECT OF CALLINRC
)@@G@@G TOC WITHOUT     @F@@@@ OPTIONS IS TO GET THE SAME SORT OF LISTING PRODRD
)@@G@@UCED BY AN @PRT,T @F@@@@ BUT WITH DELETED ELEMENTS PRECEDED BY AN ASTERIRE
)@@G@@SK AND WITH THE   @G@@@@ LISTING FORMATTED TO BETTER UTILIZE THE UNISCOPRF
)@@G@@E SCREEN.  IF OMITTED,  @A@@@@ THE FILE NAME DEFAULTS TO "TPF$."  @A@@@@RG
)@@G@@3OPTIONAL ELEMENT/VERSION MASKS     @G@@@@     "ELTMASK" AND "VERMASK" ARH
)@@G@@RE OPTIONAL 1-12 CHARACTER NAMES WHICH ARE@H@@@@ USED AS TESTS FOR PRINTRI
)@@G@@ING ENTRIES IN A TABLE.  IF "ELTMASK" IS PRESENT,     @G@@@@ TOC WILL PRRJ
)@@G@@INT ONLY ENTRIES WHICH MASK SUCCESSFULLY WITH "ELTMASK".    @G@@@@ IN OTRK
)@@G@@HER WORDS, IF "ELTMASK" IS GIVEN AS "DA", TOC WILL ONLY PRINT     @F@@@@RL
)@@G@@ ENTRIES FROM THE SELECTED TABLE WHICH BEGIN WITH "DA".  THUS THE @G@@@@RM
)@@G@@ ELEMENTS (FOR EXAMPLE) "DA", "DA$$$", AND "DAVEY" WOULD ALL BE LISTED  RN
)@@G@@@F@@@@ IF "DA" WAS GIVEN AS "ELTMASK".  THIS MASK FEATURE WORKS WITH ANYRO
)@@G@@@E@@@@ OF THE PROGRAM FILE'S TABLES, NOT JUST THE ELEMENT TABLE.  @[@@@@RP
)@@G@@0     @F@@@@     "VERMASK" FUNCTIONS WITH OR WITHOUT ALSO SPECIFYING "ELRQ
)@@G@@TMASK"@F@@@@ BUT ONLY APPLIES TO THE ELEMENT TABLE SINCE ONLY ELEMENTS ARR
)@@G@@RE    @ @@@@ ALLOWED TO HAVE VERSIONS.    @]@@@@3OPTIONS    @#@@@@2AVAILRS
)@@G@@ABLE OPTIONS@B@@@@      THE OPTIONS AVAILABLE FOR TOC ARE:  @[@@@@SPACE RT
)@@G@@@F@@@@      B - BATCH MODE FORMAT.  TOC FORMATS THE OUTPUT TO FIT ON    RU
)@@G@@@F@@@@          THE PRINTER PAGE INSTEAD OF THE SCOPE SCREEN.  TOC DOES RV
)@@G@@@F@@@@          NOT PAUSE AFTER A FULL SCREEN BUT INSTEAD PROCEEDS TO   RW
)@@G@@@E@@@@          THE END OF THE TABLE BEING PRINTED AND STOPS.     @F@@@@RX
)@@G@@          THIS OPTION IS IMPLEMENTED IF TOC IS CALLED IN A BATCH  @F@@@@RY
)@@G@@          RUN AND TAKES PRIORITY OVER ANY OTHER OPTION IF TOC IS  @E@@@@RZ
)@@G@@          CALLED IN A DEMAND RUN.  THIS OPTION IS USEFUL FOR@E@@@@      SA
)@@G@@    GETTING A LISTING WHILE BREAKPOINTED AT THE SCOPE.@[@@@@SPACE @F@@@@SB
)@@G@@      E - ENTRY POINT TABLE.  TOC PRODUCES A LISTING OF THE FILE'S@G@@@@SC
)@@G@@          ENTRY POINT TABLE INSTEAD OF THE ELEMENT TABLE.  THE NAME     SD
)@@G@@@F@@@@          OF THE ENTRY POINT IS GIVEN, PRECEDED BY AN ASTERISK IF SE
)@@G@@@F@@@@          DELETED, AND FOLLOWED BY THE SEQUENCE NUMBER OF THE     SF
)@@G@@@B@@@@          ELEMENT IN WHICH IT OCCURS.     @[@@@@SPACE @G@@@@      SG
)@@G@@P - THIS SPECIFIES THAT THE ASSEMBLER PROCEDURE TABLE ENTRIES     @F@@@@SH
)@@G@@          ARE TO BE PRINTED.  THE FORMAT IS THE SAME AS FOR THE   @ @@@@SI
)@@G@@          ENTRY POINT TABLE.  @[@@@@SPACE @F@@@@      F - THIS SPECIFIESSJ
)@@G@@ THAT THE FORTRAN PROCEDURE TABLE ENTRIES @F@@@@          ARE TO BE PRINSK
)@@G@@TED IN THE SAME FORMAT AS THE ENTRY POINT @#@@@@          TABLE.  @[@@@@SL
)@@G@@SPACE @F@@@@      C - THIS OPTION SPECIFIES THAT THE COBOL PROCEDURE TABSM
)@@G@@LE    @F@@@@          ENTRIES ARE TO BE PRINTED.  AGAIN, THE ENTRY POINTSN
)@@G@@ TABLE@E@@@@          FORMAT IS USED, WITH ONE EXCEPTION.  IF THE COBOL SO
)@@G@@@F@@@@          PROCEDURE NAME EXCEEDS 12 CHARACTERS, AN ASTERISK IS    SP
)@@G@@@F@@@@          APPENDED TO THE FIRST 12 CHARACTERS TO INDICATE THE     SQ
)@@G@@@D@@@@          REMAINING PORTION OF THE NAME IS NOT LISTED.@[@@@@SPACE SR
)@@G@@@F@@@@ NOTE:  ALL THE ABOVE OPTIONS ARE IMPLEMENTED IN THE ORDER IN     SS
)@@G@@@F@@@@        WHICH THEY APPEAR ABOVE; I.E., B, E, P, F, AND C.  IF A   ST
)@@G@@@E@@@@        COMBINATION OF OPTIONS APPEAR, THE ABOVE ORDER WILL @C@@@@SU
)@@G@@        DETERMINE WHICH OPTIONS ARE IMPLEMENTED.@[@@@@SPACE @G@@@@     ISV
)@@G@@N ADDITION, THE "N" OPTION IS AVAILABLE.  THIS OPTION CAUSES A    @F@@@@SW
)@@G@@ SUMMARY OF THE TABLE OF CONTENTS TO BE PRINTED.  THE SUMMARY     @F@@@@SX
)@@G@@ TELLS HOW MANY ENTRIES EACH TABLE IN THE PROGRAM FILE CONTAINS   @F@@@@SY
)@@G@@ AND THE NEXT AVAILABLE SECTOR.  IF USED ALONE, THE "N" OPTION    @F@@@@SZ
)@@G@@ PRINTS THE SUMMARY AND TOC TERMINATES.  IF USED IN COMBINATION   @F@@@@TA
)@@G@@ WITH OTHER OPTIONS, TOC PROCESSES THE OTHER OPTION(S) FIRST,     @C@@@@TB
)@@G@@ AND THEN PAUSES BEFORE STARTING THE SUMMARY.   @[@@@@0     @G@@@@      TC
)@@G@@ALSO AVAILABLE ARE THE A, R, O, AND S OPTIONS, WHICH SPECIFY THAT @H@@@@TD
)@@G@@ ONLY ABSOLUTE, RELOCATABLE, OMNIBUS, OR SYMBOLIC ELEMENTS ARE TO BE LISTE
)@@G@@TED.  @G@@@@ THESE THREE OPTIONS MAY BE USED IN ANY COMBINATION WITH EACTF
)@@G@@H OTHER,    @E@@@@ WITH THE DEFAULT (NO OPTIONS SPECIFIED) BEING ALL ELETG
)@@G@@MENTS,@F@@@@ REGARDLESS OF TYPE.  THESE OPTIONS WILL NOT BE IMPLEMENTED TH
)@@G@@IF ANY@F@@@@ OF THE ABOVE-MENTIONED ENTRY POINT OR PROCEDURE OPTIONS ARETI
)@@G@@ ALSO @]@@@@ SPECIFIED. @[@@@@SPACE @F@@@@     THE FORMAT OF THE LINE PRTJ
)@@G@@ODUCED WHEN LISTING THE ELEMENT     @^@@@@ TABLE IS AS FOLLOWS:   @[@@@@TK
)@@G@@0     @C@@@@                    TYPE NAME[/VERSION][(CYCLE)]@[@@@@0     TL
)@@G@@@E@@@@     IF AN ASTERISK IS PRESENT IMMEDIATELY BEFORE THE TYPE  @F@@@@TM
)@@G@@ FIELD, IT INDICATES THAT THE ELEMENT IS MARKED FOR DELETION.     @E@@@@TN
)@@G@@ IF THE ELEMENT HAS A VERSION AND/OR CYCLE ASSOCIATED WITH  @B@@@@ IT, TTO
)@@G@@HEY WILL BE INCLUDED AS INDICATED.  @[@@@@SPACE @G@@@@     ALSO AVAILABLTP
)@@G@@E FOR USE WITH THE ELEMENT TABLE ARE THE U, D, AND L  @G@@@@ OPTIONS.  TTQ
)@@G@@HE D OPTION SPECIFIES THAT ONLY DELETED ELEMENTS ARE TO     @F@@@@ BE LITR
)@@G@@STED, WHILE THE U OPTION SPECIFIES THAT ONLY NON-DELETED    @ @@@@ ELEMETS
)@@G@@NTS ARE TO BE LISTED.   @[@@@@SPACE @G@@@@     THE L OPTION CAUSES ADDITTT
)@@G@@IONAL INFORMATION TO BE PRINTED FOR EACH  @C@@@@ ELEMENT.  THE FORMAT OFTU

)@@G@@  NSEC/SSEC  DATE  TIME  SEQ  @[@@@@SPACE @]@@@@ WHERE:     @C@@@@0     TW
)@@G@@     * INDICATES THE ELEMENT IS DELETED   @A@@@@0            (BLANK = NOTX
)@@G@@N-DELETED)  @D@@@@0       TYPE IS THE ELEMENT TYPE OR SYMBOLIC SUBTYPE  TY
)@@G@@@A@@@@0       NAME IS THE ELEMENT NAME    @A@@@@0    VERSION IS THE ELEMTZ
)@@G@@ENT VERSION @D@@@@0      CYCLE IS THE HIGHEST ELEMENT CYCLE PRESENT     UA

)@@G@@0       SSEC IS THE SECTOR ADDRESS OF THE ELEMENT TEXT@E@@@@0       DATEUC
)@@G@@ IS THE DATE THE ELEMENT WAS ADDED TO THE FILE  @E@@@@0       TIME IS THUD
)@@G@@E TIME THE ELEMENT WAS ADDED TO THE FILE  @D@@@@0        SEQ IS THE SEQUUE
)@@G@@ENCE NUMBER OF THE ELEMENT    @[@@@@0     @H@@@@     THE L, U, AND D OPTUF
)@@G@@IONS ALSO FUNCTION WITH "ELTMASK" AND/OR "VERMASK"    @G@@@@ SUCH THAT (UG
)@@G@@FOR EXAMPLE) THE USER CAN LIST ONLY DELETED ELEMENTS WHICH  @ @@@@ MATCHUH
)@@G@@ THE MASK(S) GIVEN.     @#@@@@2CHANGING OPTIONS @F@@@@      THE USER HASUI

)@@G@@ER EXECUTION HAS BEGUN. ___ IN AND THE PROGRAM W*[@@@@*SDFF*@C@@@@      VA
)@@G@@       U100 SCREEN CONTROL SUBROUTINES    @^@@@@4GENERAL INFORMATION    VB

)@@G@@@G@@@@ CALLING SEQUENCES AND PERMIT USER MANIPULATION OF THE UNISCOPE 10VD
)@@G@@0     @G@@@@ SCREEN FOR THE PURPOSES OF CONTROLLING CURSOR POSITIONING, VE
)@@G@@SCROLLING,  @D@@@@ AND SO ON.  THE SUBROUTINES ARE AVAILABLE IN S*RLIB. VF
)@@G@@@#@@@@4ENTRY POINTS     @]@@@@3ESCAPE     @B@@@@                        VG
)@@G@@     CALL ESCAPE  @@@@@@@F@@@@      THIS SUBROUTINE USES PRTCN$ TO PUT TVH
)@@G@@HE USER IN ESCAPE MODE  @F@@@@ SO THAT THE SYMBIONT DOES NO SCREEN CONTRVI
)@@G@@OL OF ITS OWN.  THIS    @F@@@@ SUBROUTINE MUST BE CALLED BEFORE ANY OTHEVJ
)@@G@@RS OR UNPREDICTABLE     @^@@@@ RESULTS WILL OCCUR.    @]@@@@3RETURN     VK
)@@G@@@B@@@@                             CALL RETURN  @@@@@@@G@@@@      THIS SVL
)@@G@@UBROUTINE RETURNS THE USER TO SYMBIONT MODE VIA PRTCN$.     @F@@@@ IF POVM
)@@G@@SSIBLE, THE USER SHOULD NOT SHIFT BACK AND FORTH INTO AND   @F@@@@ OUT OVN
)@@G@@F ESCAPE MODE SINCE THE SYMBIONT SOMETIMES DOES STRANGE     @F@@@@ THINGVO
)@@G@@S WHEN TAKING OVER CONTROL, SUCH AS ERASING THE SCREEN.     @F@@@@ IF THVP
)@@G@@IS DOES NOT MATTER, THE USER CAN SHIFT IN AND OUT OF ESCAPE @ @@@@ MODE VQ
)@@G@@AS OFTEN AS DESIRED.    @[@@@@3HOME @B@@@@                             CVR
)@@G@@ALL HOME    @@@@@@@G@@@@      THIS CALL POSITIONS THE CURSOR TO THE HOMEVS
)@@G@@ POSITION (UPPER LEFT   @ @@@@ CORNER) OF THE U100 SCREEN.  @[@@@@3ERASEVT
)@@G@@@B@@@@                             CALL ERASE   @@@@@@@F@@@@      THIS CVU
)@@G@@ALL ERASES THE ENTIRE SCREEN FROM THE CURRENT CURSOR  @A@@@@ POSITION TOVV
)@@G@@ THE END OF THE DISPLAY.@[@@@@3BLANK@B@@@@                             CVW
)@@G@@ALL BLANK   @@@@@@@G@@@@      THIS CALL ERASES FROM THE CURRENT CURSOR PVX
)@@G@@OSITION TO THE END OF   @C@@@@ THE LINE ON WHICH THE CURSOR IS POSITIONEVY
)@@G@@D.    @]@@@@3HOMERS     @B@@@@                             CALL HOMERS  VZ
)@@G@@@@@@@@@F@@@@     THIS CALL COMBINES THE FUNCTIONS OF "HOME" AND "ERASE" WA
)@@G@@INTO  @]@@@@ ONE CALL.  @]@@@@3INSERT     @B@@@@                        WB
)@@G@@     CALL INSERT  @@@@@@@F@@@@      THIS CALL CAUSES THE SCREEN TO SCROLWC
)@@G@@L DOWN ONE LINE FROM THE@B@@@@ LINE ON WHICH THE CURSOR IS POSITIONED.  WD
)@@G@@@]@@@@3DELETE     @B@@@@                             CALL DELETE  @@@@@@WE
)@@G@@@F@@@@      THIS CALL CAUSES THE SCREEN TO SCROLL UP ONE LINE TO THE    WF
)@@G@@@B@@@@ LINE ON WHICH THE CURSOR IS POSITIONED.  @@@@@@@F@@@@ NOTE: INSERWG
)@@G@@T AND DELETE WILL ALLOW TITLES TO BE PLACED AT THE    @F@@@@ TOP OF THE WH
)@@G@@DISPLAY AND TO REMAIN THERE WHILE CAUSING THE SCREEN  @B@@@@ TO SCROLL UWI
)@@G@@P OR DOWN BENEATH THE TITLE.  @[@@@@3CR   @A@@@@                        WJ
)@@G@@     CALL CR@@@@@@@G@@@@      THIS CALL CAUSES A CARRIAGE RETURN TO TAKEWK
)@@G@@ PLACE.  THE CURSOR IS  @F@@@@ POSITIONED TO THE START OF THE NEXT LOWERWL
)@@G@@ LINE ON THE SCREEN.    @]@@@@3CURSOR     @C@@@@                    CALLWM
)@@G@@ CURSOR(LINE,COLUMN)    @@@@@@@F@@@@      THIS CALL WILL POSITION THE CUWN
)@@G@@RSOR TO THE LINE AND COLUMN   @F@@@@ SPECIFIED.  THE CURSOR WILL REMAIN WO
)@@G@@THERE UNTIL MOVED AGAIN EITHER@D@@@@ BY A DELIBERATE MOVE OR BY A WRITE WP
)@@G@@OR PRINT FUNCTION.@]@@@@3SETTAB     @C@@@@                       CALL SEWQ
)@@G@@TTAB(LINE,COLUMN) @@@@@@@F@@@@      THIS CALL DOES THE SAME THING AS "CUWR
)@@G@@RSOR" EXCEPT THAT A TAB @F@@@@ STOP IS INSERTED IN THE COORDINATES GIVENWS
)@@G@@.  WHEN THE TAB FUNCTION@G@@@@ IS INITIATED, THE CURSOR WILL BE POSITIONWT
)@@G@@ED TO THE SPACE IMMEDIATELY   @ @@@@ FOLLOWING THE TAB CHARACTER. @]@@@@WU
)@@G@@3SETSOE     @C@@@@                      CALL SETSOE(LINE,COLUMN)  @@@@@@WV
)@@G@@@G@@@@      THIS CALL FUNCTIONS IN THE SAME WAY AS "CURSOR" EXCEPT THAT WW
)@@G@@AFTER @G@@@@ POSITIONING THE CURSOR, IT INSERTS A START OF ENTRY (SOE) CWX
)@@G@@HARACTER    @F@@@@ AT THE COORDINATES SPECIFIED.  THIS LEAVES THE CURSORWY
)@@G@@ POSITIONED @E@@@@ IMMEDIATELY AFTER THE SOE IN POSITION (LINE,COLUMN+1)WZ
)@@G@@.     @]@@@@3PUTTAB     @B@@@@                             CALL PUTTAB  XA
)@@G@@@@@@@@@F@@@@      THIS CALL INSERTS A TAB STOP CHARACTER AT THE CURRENT XB
)@@G@@CURSOR@F@@@@ POSITION AND MOVES THE CURSOR TO THE NEXT COLUMN POSITION IXC
)@@G@@N THE @#@@@@ CURRENT LINE.    @]@@@@3PUTSOE     @B@@@@                  XD
)@@G@@           CALL PUTSOE  @@@@@@@F@@@@      THIS SUBROUTINE FUNCTIONS EXACXE
)@@G@@TLY LIKE PUTTAB EXCEPT THAT IT@C@@@@ INSERTS A SOE CHARACTER INSTEAD OF XF
)@@G@@A TAB STOP. @[@@@@3TAB  @B@@@@                             CALL TAB     XG
)@@G@@@@@@@@@F@@@@      THIS CALL CAUSES THE CURSOR TO BE POSITIONED TO THE SPXH
)@@G@@ACE   @F@@@@ IMMEDIATELY FOLLOWING THE NEXT TAB STOP ON THE SCREEN. IF TXI
)@@G@@HERE  @F@@@@ ARE NO STOPS BETWEEN THE CURSOR AND THE END OF THE DISPLAY,XJ
)@@G@@ THE  @A@@@@ CURSOR IS SENT TO HOME POSITION.   @]@@@@3TABSOE     @B@@@@XK
)@@G@@                             CALL TABSOE  @@@@@@@F@@@@      THIS CALL ISXL
)@@G@@ SIMILAR TO "TAB" EXCEPT THAT AFTER TABBING IT  @E@@@@ INSERTS A SOE CHAXM
)@@G@@RACTER AT THE CURRENT CURSOR POSITION.    @]@@@@3LBLINK     @B@@@@      XN
)@@G@@                       CALL LBLINK  @@@@@@@G@@@@     THIS CALL INSERTS AXO
)@@G@@ LEFT-BLINK CHARACTER AT THE CURRENT CURSOR     @]@@@@ POSITION.  @]@@@@XP
)@@G@@3RBLINK     @B@@@@                             CALL RBLINK  @@@@@@@G@@@@XQ
)@@G@@     THIS CALL INSERTS A RIGHT-BLINK CHARACTER AT THE CURRENT CURSOR    XR
)@@G@@@]@@@@ POSITION.  @[@@@@3BLINK@D@@@@                CALL BLINK(LINE,COLUXS
)@@G@@MN,NUMBER,LOR)    @@@@@@@F@@@@     THIS CALL PRINTS A LINE OF (NUMBER) BXT
)@@G@@LINK CHARACTERS STARTING@F@@@@ AT CURSOR POSITION (LINE, COLUMN).  IF LOXU
)@@G@@R IS 0, LEFT BLINKS WILL@E@@@@ BE GENERATED; IF LOR IS 1, RIGHT BLINKS WXV
)@@G@@ILL BE PRINTED.   @[@@@@3SCANX@C@@@@                             CALL SCXW
)@@G@@ANX(NUMBER) @@@@@@@D@@@@     THERE ARE FOUR SCAN ENTRY POINTS, AS FOLLOWXX
)@@G@@S:    @@@@@@@D@@@@          SCANU - MOVES THE CURSOR UP (NUMBER) LINES  XY
)@@G@@@D@@@@          SCAND - MOVES THE CURSOR DOWN (NUMBER) LINES@E@@@@      XZ
)@@G@@    SCANL - MOVES THE CURSOR LEFT (NUMBER) SPACES     @E@@@@          SCYA
)@@G@@ANR - MOVES THE CURSOR RIGHT (NUMBER) SPACES    @@@@@@@C@@@@ NOTE:  SCANYB
)@@G@@X ITSELF IS NOT AN ENTRY POINT.     @[@@@@3XMIT @B@@@@                  YC
)@@G@@           CALL XMIT    @@@@@@@F@@@@     THIS CALL CAUSES THE TRANSMIT FYD
)@@G@@UNCTION OF THE UNISCOPE TO BE @F@@@@ ACTIVATED JUST AS IF THE USER HAD PYE
)@@G@@RESSED THE "TRANSMIT" BUTTON. @F@@@@ A SUBSEQUENT READ WILL PICK UP THE YF
)@@G@@INFORMATION FROM THE SCREEN   @C@@@@ JUST AS IN A NORMAL USER/PROGRAM INYG
)@@G@@TERACTION.  @]@@@@3SETSCR     @F@@@@                CALL SETSCR(HOMEY,HOYH
)@@G@@MEX,INSY,INSX,UPORD,SOESW)    @@@@@@@F@@@@     THIS CALL ALLOWS THE USERYI
)@@G@@ TO CHANGE THE STANDARD SCROLLING   @F@@@@ PARAMETERS FOR USE WITH THE EYJ
)@@G@@NTRY POINT "SCROLL".  THE VALUES    @^@@@@ OF THE ARGUMENTS ARE:  @[@@@@YK
)@@G@@SPACE @E@@@@       HOMEY - LINE COORDINATE OF "HOME" POSITION ON SCREEN YL
)@@G@@@F@@@@       HOMEX - COLUMN COORDINATE OF "HOME" POSITION ON SCREEN     YM
)@@G@@@F@@@@        INSY - LINE COORDINATE OF "INSERT" POSITION ON SCREEN     YN
)@@G@@@F@@@@        INSX - COLUMN COORDINATE OF "INSERT" POSITION ON SCREEN   YO
)@@G@@@A@@@@       UPORD - SCROLL DIRECTION     @ @@@@               0 = SCROLYP
)@@G@@L UP  @ @@@@               1 = SCROLL DOWN@ @@@@       SOESW - SOE INDICYQ
)@@G@@ATOR  @E@@@@               0 = PUT SOE AT INSERT POINT AFTER SCROLLING  YR
)@@G@@@F@@@@               1 = DO NOT PUT SOE AT INSERT POINT AFTER SCROLLING YS
)@@G@@@]@@@@3SCROLL     @B@@@@                             CALL SCROLL  @[@@@@YT
)@@G@@SPACE @F@@@@     THIS CALL WILL CAUSE THE SCREEN TO SCROLL ACCORDING TO YU
)@@G@@THE   @F@@@@ PARAMETERS SET UP BY "SETSCR".  IF "SETSCR" IS NOT CALLED, YV
)@@G@@THE   @B@@@@ FOLLOWING DEFAULTS WILL TAKE EFFECT:     @[@@@@SPACE @B@@@@YW
)@@G@@     HOME POSITION IS LINE 1, COLUMN 1.   @B@@@@     INSERT POSITION IS YX
)@@G@@LINE 11, COLUMN 1.@ @@@@     SCROLL DIRECTION IS UP.  @G@@@@     THE SOEYY
)@@G@@ WILL BE DISPLAYED AT THE INSERT POINT AFTER SCROLLING.     @[@@@@SPACE YZ
)@@G@@@E@@@@ NOTE: "SCROLL" IS DESIGNED SUCH THAT LINES ABOVE AND BELOW @F@@@@ZA
)@@G@@0      THE "HOME" AND "INSERT" POINTS WILL BE FROZEN.  IN OTHER   @F@@@@ZB
)@@G@@0      WORDS, IF "SCROLL" IS CALLED WITH THE DEFAULT PARAMETERS,  @F@@@@ZC
)@@G@@0      LINE 12 (THE BOTTOM LINE) WILL NOT SCROLL UP WITH THE OTHER@F@@@@ZD
)@@G@@0      LINES.  THIS COULD BE USEFUL FOR PROVIDING SCALE LINES, FOR@#@@@@ZE
)@@G@@0      EXAMPLE.   ___@@^12 (THE BOTTOM LINE) WILL NOT SCROLL UP WITH THEZF
)@@G@@ OTHER@F@@@@0      LINES*[@@@@*SDFF*@^@@@@@RUN   Z477TC, 0073, Z  @]@@@@ZG
)@@G@@@ASG,A PFT. @E@@@@@HDG,P TOC:  INTERACTIVE TABLE OF CONTENTS PROCESSOR  ZH

)@@G@@RSTANDABLE  @ @@@@ THAN THE FINAL RESULT ANYHOW.@[@@@@SPACE @F@@@@      PF
)@@G@@THE ONLY PROBLEM THIS PRESENTS IS THE USE OF 'NEWCON' SGS'S @F@@@@ IN A PG
)@@G@@'PERFORM CONFIGURATION' GEN.  THE MATRIX WE USE IS THE ONE  @F@@@@ SUPPLPH
)@@G@@IED BY UNIVAC, SO IF WE HAVE CHANGED AN 'SPATH' CARD IN THE @G@@@@ CONFIPI
)@@G@@G PORTION OF THE SKELETON, WE MUST STILL DO A 'NEWCON CONNECT'.   @[@@@@PJ
)@@G@@SPACE @G@@@@      A REL TAPE, AS SUCH, IS NOT KEPT.  ALL THE FILES FOR APK
)@@G@@ PARTICULAR @E@@@@ LEVEL OF THE EXEC (SAY, 32.R1, OR 31.244) ARE KEPT ONPL

)@@G@@ TAPE USING @OUT. @[@@@@SPACE @F@@@@      USING THIS METHOD, A MAXIMUM OPP
)@@G@@F ONE TAPE (THE PRINT TAPE)   @F@@@@ IS NEEDED AT ANY TIME BY A NORMAL SPQ
)@@G@@YSGEN (EXCEPT WHEN WRITING    @F@@@@ THE BOOT TAPE, WHICH IS COPIED TO APR
)@@G@@ SECOND TAPE).  A MULTI-RUN   @F@@@@ SYSGEN WILL, OF COURSE, REQUIRE ONEPS
)@@G@@ PRINT TAPE FOR EACH RUN,     @C@@@@ IF THE PRINTOUT HAS BEEN DIRECTED TPT
)@@G@@O TAPE.     @[@@@@SPACE @E@@@@     RECENT ENHANCEMENTS HAVE BEEN MADE TOPU

)@@G@@ UNNEEDED FILES.  @[@@@@SPACE @]@@@@COLUMN 2    @F@@@@      EACH OF THE QP
